 $("#crash_rate").show();\n       $("#crash_rate").html(crash_rate_str);\n    }\n\n    $("#crash_count").hide();   \n     if (crashes > 0) {\n        $("#crash_count").show();\n catch (e) {\n        // Invalid regexp\n        return false;\n    }\n}\n\nfunction update_browser_url() {\n    var url = \'?\';\n    var params = get_params();\n    window.history.replaceState(null, "Crashes / Report", url + params);\n}\n\nvar FILTER_LABEL_STATES = [\n    \'show-all\', // Show all (with/without label)\n    \'hide\',     // Hide all with label\n    \'show-only\' // Show only with label\n];\n\n\n// *** Keyboard navigation between crashes ***\nfunction isInView() {\n    var $elem = $(this);\n    var $window = $(window);\n\n    var docViewTop = $window.scrollTop();\n    var docViewBottom = docViewTop + $window.height();\n\n    var elemTop = $elem.offset().top;\n    var elemBottom = elemTop + $elem.height();\n\n    return between(elemTop, elemBottom, docViewTop) || between(docViewTop, docViewBottom, elemTop);\n}\n\nfunction between(a, b, x) {\n    return a <= x && x <= b;\n}\n\nfunction moveToPrev(e) {\n    var prevId = $(\'.active-crash-panel\')\n            .filter(isInView)\n            .first()\n            .prevAll(\'.active-crash-panel\')\n            .first()\n            .attr(\'id\');\n\n    if (prevId) {\n        e.preventDefault();\n        window.location.hash = \'#\' + prevId;\n    }\n}\n\nfunction moveToNext(e) {\n    var nextId = $(\'.active-crash-panel\')\n            .filter(isInView)\n            .first()\n            .nextAll(\'.active-crash-panel\')\n            .first()\n            .attr(\'id\');\n    if (nextId) {\n        e.preventDefault();\n        window.location.hash = \'#\' + nextId;\n    }\n}\n\nfunction registerNavigationKeys() {\n    $(document).keydown(function(e) {\n        if ($(e.target).is(\'input, textarea\')) {\n            return;\n        }\n        var code = e.keyCode;\n        if (e.charCode && code === 0) {\n            code = e.charCode;\n        }\n        switch (code) {\n            case 40: // Arrow down\n            case 74: // j\n                moveToNext(e);\n                break;\n            case 38: // Arrow up\n            case 75: // k\n                moveToPrev(e);\n                break;\n            case 32: // Spacebar\n                if (e.shiftKey) {  // Shift+Spacebar\n                    moveToPrev(e);\n                } else {           // Just a Spacebar\n                    moveToNext(e);\n                }\n                break;\n        }\n    });\n}\n\n\n// *** End of navigation ***\n\nfunction multistate_checkbox_init(checkbox, state) {\n    multistate_checkbox_set_state(checkbox, state);\n    console.log("Setting initial state to: " + checkbox.data(\'state\'));\n\n    checkbox.change(function () {\n        var checkbox = $(this);\n        var state = checkbox.data(\'state\');\n        var pos = FILTER_LABEL_STATES.indexOf(state);\n        var next_state = FILTER_LABEL_STATES[(pos + 1) % FILTER_LABEL_STATES.length];\n        multistate_checkbox_set_state(checkbox, next_state);\n        search_server();\n    });\n}\n\nfunction multistate_checkbox_set_state(checkbox, state) {\n    checkbox.data(\'state\', state);\n\n    switch (state) {\n        // unchecked\n        case \'show-all\':\n            checkbox.prop(\'indeterminate\', false);\n            checkbox.prop(\'checked\', false);\n        break;\n\n        // indeterminate\n        case \'hide\':\n            checkbox.prop(\'indeterminate\', true);\n        break;\n\n        // checked\n        case \'show-only\':\n            checkbox.prop(\'indeterminate\', false);\n            checkbox.prop(\'checked\', true);\n        break;\n    }\n}\n\n\n$(document).ready(function() {\n\n    $(\'#report-day\').datepicker({\n        format:    \'yyyy-mm-dd\',\n        endDate:   \'2021-03-31\',\n        weekStart: };\n        url += $.param(url_params) + \'&\';\n    }\n\n    console.log("URL = " + url);\n    $.getJSON(url, function (tickets, status) {\n        if (tickets.error) {\n            console.log("failed to fetch jira tickets: %s", tickets.error);\n            return;\n        }\n\n        for (var key in tickets) {\n            var ticket = tickets[key];\n            var elements = jira_dom[key];\n            if (!elements) {\n                console.log("Can\'t find DOM element for jira key: %s", key);\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            var html = make_jira_html(ticket);\n            for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; ++i) {\n                var element = elements[i];\n                element.replaceWith(html);\n            }\n        }\n (ticket.assignee) {\n        html += " <img src=\'" + ticket.assignee_avatar + "&size=small\' class=\'avatar\'>";\n        html += " " + ticket.assignee;\n    }\n\n    if (ticket.status) {\n
